  28: function s(v: any) {
  29:   return v === null || v === undefined ? "" : String(v);
  30: }
  31: 
  32: function buildMailThreadLink(threadKey: string): string {
  33:   const params = new URLSearchParams();
  34:   if (String(threadKey || "").trim()) params.set("thread", String(threadKey || "").trim());
  35:   return `/mail-threads?${params.toString()}`;
  36: }
  37: 
  38: function loadMailHomeDraft() {
  39:   try {
  40:     const raw = localStorage.getItem(MAIL_HOME_DRAFT_KEY);
  41:     return raw ? JSON.parse(raw) : {};
  42:   } catch {
  43:     return {};
  44:   }
  45: }
  46: 
  47: function saveMailHomeDraft(next: any) {
  48:   try {
  49:     localStorage.setItem(MAIL_HOME_DRAFT_KEY, JSON.stringify(next || {}));
  50:   } catch {}
  51: }
  52: 
  53: function clearMailHomeDraft() {
  54:   try {
  55:     localStorage.removeItem(MAIL_HOME_DRAFT_KEY);
  56:   } catch {}
  57: }

  59: function previewSnippet(m: InboxRow) {
  60:   const text = s(m.body).replace(/\s+/g, " ").trim();
  61:   if (!text) return "(no preview)";
  62:   return text.length > 160 ? text.slice(0, 160) + "…" : text;
  63: }

  65: function niceDate(v: any) {
  66:   try {
  67:     return new Date(String(v || "")).toLocaleString();
  68:   } catch {
  69:     return String(v || "");
  70:   }

 147:   async function openNewestThreadForRecipient(targetUserId: string) {
 148:     try {
 149:       const res = await supabase
 150:         .from("v_my_mail_threads")
 151:         .select("*")
 152:         .order("last_message_at", { ascending: false });
 153: 
 154:       if (res.error) return;
 155: 
 156:       const rows = (res.data ?? []) as any[];
 157:       const match = rows.find((r) => {
 158:         const a = String(r?.peer_user_id || r?.other_user_id || r?.to_user_id || "");
 159:         const b = String(r?.from_user_id || "");

 161:       });
 162:

 164:         nav(`/mail-threads?thread=${encodeURIComponent(String(match.thread_key))}`);

 173:   async function sendDirectMail() {

 223:       const kindOk = !filterKind || kind === filterKind;
 224: 
 225:       const tabOk =
 226:         mailTab === "all" ? true :
 227:         mailTab === "inbox" ? direction !== "out" :
 228:         mailTab === "sent" ? direction === "out" :
 229:         mailTab === "broadcast" ? kind === "alliance_broadcast" || kind === "state_broadcast" :

 233:         `${s(m.subject)} ${s(m.body)} ${s(m.from_display_name)} ${s(m.sender_display_name)} ${s(m.peer_display_name)}`.toLowerCase();

 252:   function pickRecipient(recipientId: string) {
 253:     const id = s(recipientId);

 258:   function recipientLabel(r: RecipientRow) {
 259:     const name = s(r.display_name || r.game_name || r.user_id || r.id || "Unknown");

 264:   function prefillReply(m: InboxRow) {
 265:     const directTarget = s(m.direction) === "out"
 266:       ? ""
 267:       : "";
 268:     const subjectText = s(m.subject).trim();
 269:     const nextSubject = subjectText
 270:       ? (subjectText.toLowerCase().startsWith("re:") ? subjectText : `Re: ${subjectText}`)
 271:       : "";
 272: 
 273:     const possibleRecipient = recipients.find((r) => {
 274:       const label = recipientLabel(r);
 275:       return (
 276:         label === s(m.peer_display_name) ||
 277:         label === s(m.sender_display_name) ||
 278:         s(r.display_name) === s(m.peer_display_name) ||
 279:         s(r.display_name) === s(m.sender_display_name) ||
 280:         s(r.game_name) === s(m.peer_display_name) ||
 281:         s(r.game_name) === s(m.sender_display_name)
 282:       );
 283:     });
 284:

 288:     setStatus("Reply loaded into composer ✅");
 289:     window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: "smooth" });
 290:   }

===== FILE: .\src\pages\mail\MyMailThreadsPage.tsx =====
   1: import { useLocation, useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";
   2: import React, { useEffect, useMemo, useState } from "react";
   3: import { supabase } from "../../lib/supabaseClient";
   4: import SupportBundleButton from "../../components/system/SupportBundleButton";
   5: 
   6: type ThreadRow = {
   7:   thread_key: string;
   8:   subject: string | null;
   9:   preview: string | null;
  10:   last_from: string | null;
  11:   last_message_at: string | null;
  12:   unread_count: number;
  13: };
  14: 
  15: type MsgRow = {
  16:   thread_key: string;
  17:   from_name: string;
  18:   to_name: string;
  19:   subject_norm: string | null;
  20:   body: any;
  21:   created_at_norm: string;
  22:   from_user_id_norm: string;
  23:   to_user_id_norm: string | null;
  24: };
  25: 
  26: type PlayerOpt = { user_id: string; display_name: string; player_id: string };
  27: 
  28: function fmt(dt?: string | null) {
  29:   if (!dt) return "—";
  30:   try { return new Date(dt).toLocaleString(); } catch { return dt; }
  31: }
  32: 
  33: function isDmThread(threadKey: string) {
  34:   return String(threadKey || "").startsWith("dm:");
  35: }
  36: 
  37: function ReplyBox(props: { threadKey: string; onSent: () => void }) {
  38:   const [me, setMe] = useState<string>("");
  39:   const [peer, setPeer] = useState<{ id: string; name: string } | null>(null);
  40:   const [body, setBody] = useState<string>("");
  41:   const [status, setStatus] = useState<string>("");useEffect(() => {
  42:     (async () => {
  43:       const u = await supabase.auth.getUser();
  44:       setMe(u.data?.user?.id || "");
  45:     })();
  46:   }, []);useEffect(() => {
  47:     (async () => {
  48:       setPeer(null);
  49:       if (!props.threadKey || !isDmThread(props.threadKey) || !me) return;
  50: 
  51:       const r = await supabase
  52:         .from("v_my_mail_messages")
  53:         .select("from_user_id_norm,to_user_id_norm,from_name,to_name,thread_key,created_at_norm")
  54:         .eq("thread_key", props.threadKey)
  55:         .order("created_at_norm", { ascending: false })
  56:         .limit(50);
  57: 
  58:       if (r.error || !r.data?.length) return;
  59: 
  60:       let pid = "";
  61:       let pname = "";
  62: 
  63:       for (const m of (r.data as any[])) {
  64:         const f = String(m.from_user_id_norm || "");
  65:         const t = String(m.to_user_id_norm || "");
  66:         if (f && f !== me) { pid = f; pname = String(m.from_name || ""); break; }
  67:         if (t && t !== me) { pid = t; pname = String(m.to_name || ""); break; }
  68:       }
  69: 
  70:       if (!pid) return;
  71:       setPeer({ id: pid, name: pname || pid });
  72:     })();
  73:   }, [props.threadKey, me]);
  74: 
  75:   async function send() {
  76:     if (!peer?.id) return;
  77:     if (!body.trim()) return alert("Reply body required.");
  78: 
  79:     setStatus("Sending…");
  80:     const r = await supabase.rpc("mail_send_message", {
  81:       p_to_user_id: peer.id,
  82:       p_subject: null,
  83:       p_body: body,
  84:       p_alliance_code: null,
  85:     });
  86: 
  87:     if (r.error) { setStatus(r.error.message); return; }
  88:     setBody("");
  89:     setStatus("Sent ✅");
  90:     props.onSent();
  91:     window.setTimeout(() => setStatus(""), 900);
  92:   }
  93: 
  94:   const disabledReason = !props.threadKey
  95:     ? "No thread selected."
  96:     : !isDmThread(props.threadKey)
  97:     ? "Reply disabled for broadcast threads."
  98:     : !peer
  99:     ? "Finding peer…"
 100:     : "";
 101: 
 102:     // Realtime: reload inbox/threads when any mail_items change
 103:   useEffect(() => {
 104:     let ch: any = null;
 105:     let alive = true;
 106: 
 107:     (async () => {
 108:       const u = await supabase.auth.getUser();
 109:       const uid = u.data?.user?.id;
 110:       if (!uid || !alive) return;
 111: 
 112:       ch = supabase
 113:         .channel(`rt_mail_items_${uid}`)
 114:         .on(
 115:           "postgres_changes",
 116:           { event: "*", schema: "public", table: "mail_items" },
 117:           () => {
 118:             // debounce reload slightly to avoid rapid bursts
 119:             window.clearTimeout((window as any).__rt_mail_t);
 120:             (window as any).__rt_mail_t = window.setTimeout(() => {
 121:               try { void load(); } catch {}
 122:             }, 250);
 123:           }
 124:         )
 125:         .subscribe();
 126:     })();
 127: 
 128:     return () => {
 129:       alive = false;
 130:       try { if (ch) supabase.removeChannel(ch); } catch {}
 131:     };
 132:   }, []);
 133: 
 134: return (
 135:     <div style={{ marginTop: 12, borderTop: "1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.12)", paddingTop: 12 }}>
 136:       <div style={{ display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between", gap: 10, flexWrap: "wrap", alignItems: "center" }}>
 137:         <div style={{ fontWeight: 950 }}>Reply</div>
 138:         <div style={{ opacity: 0.8, fontSize: 12 }}>{status || (peer ? `To: ${peer.name}` : disabledReason)}</div>
 139:       </div>
 140: 
 141:       <textarea
 142:         value={body}
 143:         onChange={(e) => setBody(e.target.value)}
 144:         rows={3}
 145:         placeholder={peer ? "Write a reply…" : "Reply not available."}
 146:         style={{ width: "100%", marginTop: 8 }}
 147:         disabled={!peer}
 148:       />
 149: 
 150:       <div style={{ marginTop: 8, display: "flex", justifyContent: "flex-end" }}>
 151:         <button type="button" onClick={() => void send()} disabled={!peer}>Send Reply</button>
 152:       </div>
 153:     </div>
 154:   );
 155: }

 170:   async function loadPlayers() {
 171:     const res = await supabase
 172:       .from("v_approved_players")

 174:       .order("display_name", { ascending: true });
 175: 
 176:     if (!res.error) setPlayers((res.data ?? []) as any);
 177:   }
 178: 
 179:   async function loadThreads() {
 180:     const res = await supabase.from("v_my_mail_threads").select("*");
 181:     if (res.error) { setStatus(res.error.message); setThreads([]); return; }
 182:     const rows = (res.data ?? []) as any as ThreadRow[];
 183:     setThreads(rows);
 184:     if (!selected && rows.length) setSelected(rows[0].thread_key);
 185:   }
 186: 
 187:   async function loadMsgs(threadKey: string) {
 188:     setStatus("Loading messages…");
 189:     const res = await supabase
 190:       .from("v_my_mail_messages")
 191:       .select("*")
 192:       .eq("thread_key", threadKey)
 193:       .order("created_at_norm", { ascending: true });
 194: 
 195:     if (res.error) { setStatus(res.error.message); setMsgs([]); return; }
 196:     setMsgs((res.data ?? []) as any);
 197:     setStatus("");
 198: 
 199:     await supabase.rpc("mail_mark_thread_read", { p_thread_key: threadKey });
 200:     await loadThreads();
 201:   }
 202: 
 203:   useEffect(() => {
 204:     const params = new URLSearchParams();
 205:     if (String(selected || "").trim()) params.set("thread", String(selected || "").trim());
 206:     const qs = params.toString();
 207:     window.history.replaceState(null, "", qs ? `/mail-threads?${qs}` : "/mail-threads");
 208:   }, [selected]);
 209: 
 210:   useEffect(() => {
 211:     void loadPlayers();
 212:     void loadThreads();
 213:     // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
 214:   }, []);
 215: 
 216:   useEffect(() => {
 217:     const params = new URLSearchParams();
 218:     if (String(selected || "").trim()) params.set("thread", String(selected || "").trim());

 221:   }, [selected]);
 222:

 337:                   <div style={{ opacity: 0.7, fontSize: 12 }}>{fmt(m.created_at_norm)}</div>
 338:                 </div>
 339:                 <div style={{ marginTop: 8 }}><MailMessageBody body={String(m.body ?? "")} /></div>
 340:               </div>
 341:             ))}
 342:             {!msgs.length ? <div style={{ opacity: 0.8 }}>No messages in this thread.</div> : null}
 343:           </div>
 344: 
 345:           <ReplyBox
 346:             threadKey={selected || ""}
 347:             onSent={() => { if (selected) void loadMsgs(selected); }}
 348:           />
 349:         </div>
 350:       </div>
 351:     </div>
 352:   );
 353: }

===== FILE: .\src\pages\mail\MyMailInboxPage.tsx =====
   1: import React, { useEffect, useMemo, useState } from "react";
   2: import { useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";
   3: import { supabase } from "../../lib/supabaseBrowserClient";
   4: import { useTranslation } from "react-i18next";
   5: 
   6: type Recipient = { user_id: string; display_name: string };
   7: 
   8: type MailItem = {
   9:   id: string;
  10:   created_at: string;
  11:   kind: "direct" | "alliance_broadcast" | "state_broadcast";
  12:   subject: string;
  13:   body: string;
  14: 
  15:   sender_display_name?: string | null;
  16: 
  17:   direction?: "in" | "out" | null;
  18:   peer_user_id?: string | null;
  19:   peer_display_name?: string | null;
  20: 
  21:   thread_id?: string | null;
  22: };
  23: 
  24: async function copyToClipboard(text: string): Promise<boolean> {
  25:   try { await navigator.clipboard.writeText(text); return true; }
  26:   catch { return false; }
  27: }
  28: 
  29: export default function MyMailInboxPage() {
  30:   const nav = useNavigate();
  31:   const { t } = useTranslation();
  32:   const [userId, setUserId] = useState<string>("");
  33:   const [items, setItems] = useState<MailItem[]>([]);
  34:   const [status, setStatus] = useState("");
  35:   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  36: 
  37:   const [recipients, setRecipients] = useState<Recipient[]>([]);
  38:   const [toUserId, setToUserId] = useState("");
  39:   const [subject, setSubject] = useState("");
  40:   const [body, setBody] = useState("");
  41: 
  42:   const [filterKind, setFilterKind] = useState<string>("");
  43:   const [q, setQ] = useState("");
  44: 
  45:   useEffect(() => {
  46:     let mounted = true;
  47:     (async () => {
  48:       const { data } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
  49:       const uid = data.user?.id ?? "";
  50:       if (!mounted) return;
  51:       setUserId(uid);
  52:       if (uid) {
  53:         await loadRecipients();
  54:         await refresh();
  55:       }
  56:     })();
  57: 
  58:     return () => { mounted = false; };
  59:   }, []);
  60: 
  61:   async function loadRecipients() {
  62:     const res = await supabase.rpc("list_dm_recipients");
  63:     if (!res.error) setRecipients((res.data ?? []) as any);
  64:   }
  65: 
  66:   async function refresh() {
  67:     setLoading(true);
  68:     setStatus(t("common.loading"));
  69:     const res = await supabase.from("v_my_mail_inbox").select("*").order("created_at", { ascending: false }).limit(200);
  70:     if (res.error) { setStatus(res.error.message); setLoading(false); return; }
  71:     setItems((res.data ?? []) as any);
  72:     setStatus("");
  73:     setLoading(false);
  74:   }
  75: 
  76:   async function sendDirect() {
  77:     const to = toUserId.trim();
  78:     const b = body.trim();
  79:     if (!to || !b) return alert("Recipient and body required.");
  80: 
  81:     setLoading(true);
  82:     setStatus(t("common.sending"));
  83: 
  84:     const res = await supabase.rpc("send_direct_message", {
  85:       p_to_user_id: to,
  86:       p_subject: subject.trim(),
  87:       p_body: b,
  88:     });
  89: 
  90:     if (res.error) { setStatus(res.error.message); setLoading(false); return; }
  91: 
  92:     setToUserId("");
  93:     setSubject("");
  94:     setBody("");
  95: 
  96:     await refresh();
  97:     setStatus(t("common.sent"));
  98:     window.setTimeout(() => setStatus(""), 1200);
  99:     setLoading(false);
 100:   }
 101: 
 102:   const filtered = useMemo(() => {
 103:     const qq = q.trim().toLowerCase();
 104:     return items.filter((m) => {
 105:       if (filterKind && m.kind !== filterKind) return false;
 106:       if (!qq) return true;
 107:       const hay = `${m.subject} ${m.body} ${m.kind} ${m.sender_display_name ?? ""} ${m.peer_display_name ?? ""}`.toLowerCase();
 108:       return hay.includes(qq);
 109:     });
 110:   }, [items, filterKind, q]);
 111: 
 112:   function whoLine(m: MailItem) {
 113:     const sender = m.sender_display_name || "Unknown";
 114:     if (m.kind !== "direct") return `${t("mailInbox.fromLabel")}: ${sender}`;
 115:     if (m.direction === "out") return `${t("mailInbox.toLabel")}: ${m.peer_display_name ?? "Unknown"}`;
 116:     return `${t("mailInbox.fromLabel")}: ${sender}`;
 117:   }
 118: 
 119:   return (
 120:     <div style={{ padding: 16, maxWidth: 1200, margin: "0 auto" }}>
 121:       <div style={{ display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between", gap: 12, flexWrap: "wrap", alignItems: "center" }}>
 122:         <h1 style={{ fontSize: 22, fontWeight: 900, margin: 0 }}>{t("mailInbox.title")}</h1>
 123:         <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 8, flexWrap: "wrap" }}>
 124:           <button className="zombie-btn" type="button" onClick={() => nav("/mail")}>Mail Home</button>
 125:           <button className="zombie-btn" type="button" onClick={() => nav("/mail-threads")}>Threads</button>
 126:           <button className="zombie-btn" type="button" onClick={() => nav("/owner/mail-broadcast")}>Broadcast</button>
 127:         </div>
 128:       </div>
 129:       <div style={{ opacity: 0.8, marginTop: 6 }}>
 130:         {userId ? "✅" : ""}{loading ? " • " + t("common.loading") : ""}{status ? " • " + status : ""}
 131:       </div>
 132: 
 133:       <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 10, flexWrap: "wrap", marginTop: 12, alignItems: "center" }}>
 134:         <button disabled={!userId || loading} onClick={refresh}>{t("common.reload")}</button>
 135:         <button disabled={!userId || loading} onClick={loadRecipients}>{t("mailInbox.refreshRecipients")}</button>
 136: 
 137:         <select value={filterKind} onChange={(e) => setFilterKind(e.target.value)}>
 138:           <option value="">{t("mailInbox.filterAll")}</option>
 139:           <option value="direct">{t("mailInbox.filterDirect")}</option>
 140:           <option value="alliance_broadcast">{t("mailInbox.filterAllianceBroadcast")}</option>
 141:           <option value="state_broadcast">{t("mailInbox.filterStateBroadcast")}</option>
 142:         </select>
 143: 
 144:         <input value={q} onChange={(e) => setQ(e.target.value)} placeholder={t("mailInbox.searchPlaceholder")} />
 145:         <div style={{ opacity: 0.75 }}>{t("mailInbox.showing", { count: filtered.length })}</div>
 146:       </div>
 147: 
 148:       <hr style={{ margin: "16px 0", opacity: 0.3 }} />
 149: 
 150:       <div style={{ border: "1px solid #333", borderRadius: 12, overflow: "hidden" }}>
 151:         <div style={{ padding: 12, borderBottom: "1px solid #333", fontWeight: 900 }}>{t("mailInbox.sendDirectTitle")}</div>
 152:         <div style={{ padding: 12, display: "grid", gap: 10 }}>
 153:           <div>
 154:             <div style={{ opacity: 0.75, fontSize: 12 }}>{t("mailInbox.recipientApprovedLabel")}</div>
 155:             <select value={toUserId} onChange={(e) => setToUserId(e.target.value)}>
 156:               <option value="">{t("mailThreads.selectPlayer")}</option>
 157:               {recipients.map((r) => <option key={r.user_id} value={r.user_id}>{r.display_name}</option>)}
 158:             </select>
 159:           </div>
 160: 
 161:           <input value={subject} onChange={(e) => setSubject(e.target.value)} placeholder={t("mailInbox.subjectOptional")} />
 162:           <textarea value={body} onChange={(e) => setBody(e.target.value)} rows={4} placeholder={t("mailInbox.bodyPlaceholder")} />
 163: 
 164:           <div style={{ display: "flex", justifyContent: "flex-end" }}>
 165:             <button disabled={!userId || loading || !toUserId || !body.trim()} onClick={sendDirect}>{t("mailThreads.send")}</button>
 166:           </div>
 167:         </div>
 168:       </div>
 169: 
 170:       <hr style={{ margin: "16px 0", opacity: 0.3 }} />
 171: 
 172:       <div style={{ display: "grid", gap: 12 }}>
 173:         {filtered.map((m) => (
 174:           <div key={m.id} style={{ border: "1px solid #333", borderRadius: 12, overflow: "hidden" }}>
 175:             <div style={{ padding: 12, borderBottom: "1px solid #333", display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between", gap: 10, flexWrap: "wrap" }}>
 176:               <div>
 177:                 <div style={{ fontWeight: 900 }}>[{m.kind}] {m.subject || "(no subject)"}</div>
 178:                 <div style={{ opacity: 0.75, fontSize: 12 }}>
 179:                   {new Date(m.created_at).toLocaleString()} • {whoLine(m)}
 180:                 </div>
 181:               </div>
 182:               <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 8 }}>
 183:                 <button onClick={async () => alert((await copyToClipboard(m.body)) ? t("common.copied") : t("common.copyFailed"))}>{t("common.copy")}</button>
 184:                 <button onClick={async () => alert((await copyToClipboard(JSON.stringify(m, null, 2))) ? t("common.copied") : t("common.copyFailed"))}>JSON</button>
 185:               </div>
 186:             </div>
 187:             <div style={{ padding: 12, whiteSpace: "pre-wrap" }}>{m.body}</div>
 188:           </div>
 189:         ))}
 190:         {filtered.length === 0 ? <div style={{ opacity: 0.7 }}>{t("mailInbox.noMailYet")}</div> : null}
 191:       </div>
 192:     </div>
 193:   );
 194: }

===== FILE: .\src\pages\owner\OwnerCommandCenterPage.tsx =====
   1: import { useEffect, useMemo, useState } from "react";
   2: import { Link } from "react-router-dom";
   3: import { supabase } from "../../lib/supabaseClient";
   4: import OwnerCard from "../../components/owner/OwnerCard";
   5: 
   6: type AllianceRow = { code: string; name?: string | null; enabled?: boolean | null };
   7: type DiscordRow = { alliance_id?: string | null; webhook_url?: string | null; role_id?: string | null; enabled?: boolean | null };
   8: type HealthState = {
   9:   sessionUserId: string | null;
  10:   lastRefreshed: string | null;
  11:   pendingRequests: number | null;
  12:   alliances: number | null;
  13:   players: number | null;
  14:   memberships: number | null;
  15:   events: number | null;
  16:   reminderLastAt: string | null;
  17:   discordConfigured: number | null;
  18:   discordMissing: number | null;
  19:   errors: string[];
  20: };
  21: 
  22: function maskWebhook(url?: string | null) {
  23:   if (!url) return "—";
  24:   // show only host + last 6 chars
  25:   try {
  26:     const u = new URL(url);
  27:     const tail = url.slice(-6);
  28:     return `${u.host}/…${tail}`;
  29:   } catch {
  30:     const tail = url.slice(-6);
  31:     return `…${tail}`;
  32:   }
  33: }
  34: 
  35: async function countTable(table: string, filter?: (q: any) => any): Promise<number | null> {
  36:   try {
  37:     let q = supabase.from(table).select("*", { count: "exact", head: true });
  38:     if (filter) q = filter(q);
  39:     const res = await q;
  40:     if (res.error) return null;
  41:     return typeof res.count === "number" ? res.count : 0;
  42:   } catch {
  43:     return null;
  44:   }
  45: }
  46: 
  47: export default function OwnerCommandCenterPage() {
  48:   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  49:   const [health, setHealth] = useState<HealthState>({
  50:     sessionUserId: null,
  51:     lastRefreshed: null,
  52:     pendingRequests: null,
  53:     alliances: null,
  54:     players: null,
  55:     memberships: null,
  56:     events: null,
  57:     reminderLastAt: null,
  58:     discordConfigured: null,
  59:     discordMissing: null,
  60:     errors: [],
  61:   });
  62: 
  63:   const [alliances, setAlliances] = useState<AllianceRow[]>([]);
  64:   const [discord, setDiscord] = useState<DiscordRow[]>([]);
  65: 
  66:   const refresh = async () => {
  67:     setLoading(true);
  68:     const errors: string[] = [];
  69: 
  70:     // Session
  71:     const u = await supabase.auth.getUser();
  72:     const sessionUserId = u.data?.user?.id ?? null;
  73: 
  74:     // Counts (best-effort; RLS may restrict if owner policy isn’t active)
  75:     const pendingRequests = await countTable("access_requests", (q) => q.eq("status", "pending"));
  76:     const alliancesCount = await countTable("alliances");
  77:     const playersCount = await countTable("players");
  78:     const membershipsCount = await countTable("player_alliances");
  79:     const eventsCount = await countTable("alliance_events");
  80: 
  81:     // Reminder “activity”: latest reminder_logs.created_at (best effort)
  82:     let reminderLastAt: string | null = null;
  83:     try {
  84:       const r = await supabase
  85:         .from("reminder_logs")
  86:         .select("created_at")
  87:         .order("created_at", { ascending: false })
  88:         .limit(1);
  89:       reminderLastAt = (r.data && r.data[0] && (r.data[0] as any).created_at) ? (r.data[0] as any).created_at : null;
  90:     } catch {
  91:       reminderLastAt = null;
  92:     }
  93: 
  94:     // Alliances list (for jump links)
  95:     try {
  96:       const resA = await supabase.from("alliances").select("code,name,enabled").order("code", { ascending: true });
  97:       if (!resA.error) {
  98:         setAlliances((resA.data || []) as any);
  99:       } else {
 100:         const msg = (resA.error.message || "").toLowerCase();
 101:         if (msg.includes("enabled")) {
 102:           const resB = await supabase.from("alliances").select("code,name").order("code", { ascending: true });
 103:           if (!resB.error) setAlliances(((resB.data || []) as any).map((x: any) => ({ ...x, enabled: true })));
 104:           else errors.push(resB.error.message);
 105:         } else {
 106:           errors.push(resA.error.message);
 107:         }
 108:       }
 109:     } catch (e: any) {
 110:       errors.push(e?.message || "Failed to load alliances");
 111:     }
 112: 
 113:     // Discord settings coverage (masked)
 114:     let discordConfigured: number | null = null;
 115:     let discordMissing: number | null = null;
 116:     try {
 117:       const resA = await supabase
 118:         .from("alliance_discord_settings")
 119:         .select("alliance_id,webhook_url,role_id,enabled")
 120:         .order("alliance_id", { ascending: true });
 121: 
 122:       if (!resA.error) {
 123:         const rows = (resA.data || []) as any[];
 124:         setDiscord(rows);
 125:         const enabledRows = rows.filter((r) => r.enabled !== false);
 126:         discordConfigured = enabledRows.filter((r) => !!r.webhook_url && String(r.webhook_url).trim() !== "").length;
 127:         discordMissing = enabledRows.filter((r) => !r.webhook_url || String(r.webhook_url).trim() === "").length;
 128:       } else {
 129:         // fallback: select *
 130:         const resB = await supabase.from("alliance_discord_settings").select("*").limit(500);
 131:         if (!resB.error) {
 132:           const rows = (resB.data || []) as any[];
 133:           setDiscord(rows);
 134:           const enabledRows = rows.filter((r) => r.enabled !== false);
 135:           discordConfigured = enabledRows.filter((r) => !!r.webhook_url && String(r.webhook_url).trim() !== "").length;
 136:           discordMissing = enabledRows.filter((r) => !r.webhook_url || String(r.webhook_url).trim() === "").length;
 137:         } else {
 138:           errors.push(resB.error.message);
 139:         }
 140:       }
 141:     } catch (e: any) {
 142:       errors.push(e?.message || "Failed to load discord settings");
 143:     }
 144: 
 145:     setHealth({
 146:       sessionUserId,
 147:       lastRefreshed: new Date().toISOString(),
 148:       pendingRequests,
 149:       alliances: alliancesCount,
 150:       players: playersCount,
 151:       memberships: membershipsCount,
 152:       events: eventsCount,
 153:       reminderLastAt,
 154:       discordConfigured,
 155:       discordMissing,
 156:       errors,
 157:     });
 158: 
 159:     setLoading(false);
 160:   };
 161: 
 162:   useEffect(() => {
 163:     refresh();
 164:     // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
 165:   }, []);
 166: 
 167:   const reminderStatus = useMemo(() => {
 168:     if (!health.reminderLastAt) return { label: "Unknown", ok: false };
 169:     const t = new Date(health.reminderLastAt).getTime();
 170:     const ageMin = Math.floor((Date.now() - t) / 60000);
 171:     // Reminder logs only happen when reminders are sent; so this is “activity”, not a heartbeat.
 172:     return ageMin <= 60
 173:       ? { label: `Active (last send ${ageMin}m ago)`, ok: true }
 174:       : { label: `No sends in ${ageMin}m`, ok: false };
 175:   }, [health.reminderLastAt]);
 176: 
 177:   const logout = async () => {
 178:     await supabase.auth.signOut();
 179:     window.location.href = "/";
 180:   };
 181: 
 182:   const pill = (text: string, ok?: boolean) => (
 183:     <span
 184:       style={{
 185:         fontSize: 12,
 186:         padding: "3px 8px",
 187:         borderRadius: 999,
 188:         border: "1px solid #333",
 189:         background: ok ? "rgba(0,255,140,0.08)" : "rgba(255,80,80,0.08)",
 190:         color: ok ? "#8cffc7" : "#ff9c9c",
 191:       }}
 192:     >
 193:       {text}
 194:     </span>
 195:   );
 196: 
 197:   return (
 198:     <div style={{ padding: 24 }}>
 199:       <div style={{ display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between", gap: 10, flexWrap: "wrap", alignItems: "center" }}>
 200:         <div>
 201:           <h2 style={{ margin: 0 }}>🧟 Owner Command Center</h2>
 202:       <div style={{ marginTop: 10 }}><a href="/owner/player-intake" style={{ textDecoration: "none" }}>🧪 Player Intake (pre-register)</a></div>
 203:           <div style={{ marginTop: 6, fontSize: 12, opacity: 0.75 }}>
 204:             One page to run the whole state. (Health + links + quick jumps)
 205:           </div>
 206:         </div>
 207: 
 208:         <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 10, flexWrap: "wrap", alignItems: "center" }}>
 209:           <button onClick={refresh} disabled={loading}>{loading ? "Refreshing…" : "↻ Refresh"}</button>
 210:           <button onClick={logout}>🚪 Logout</button>
 211:         </div>
 212:       </div>
 213: 
 214:       {/* Quick Links */}
 215:       <div style={{ marginTop: 16, display: "grid", gap: 12, gridTemplateColumns: "repeat(auto-fit, minmax(260px, 1fr))" }}>
 216:         <OwnerCard title="Owner Tools" icon="🛠️">
 217:           <div style={{ display: "grid", gap: 8 }}>
 218:             <Link to="/owner/requests-provision">✅ Requests — Approve + Provision</Link>
 219:             <Link to="/owner/players">👤 Players</Link>
 220:             <Link to="/owner/players-link">🔗 Players — Link/Unlink Auth</Link>
 221:             <Link to="/owner/membership">🧬 Membership Manager</Link>
 222:             <Link to="/owner/alliances">🏷️ Alliances (Add/Edit/Delete)</Link>
 223:             <Link to="/dashboard/WOC/discord-webhooks">📣 Discord Settings (Owner Dashboard)</Link>
 224:           </div>
 225:         </OwnerCard>
 226: 
 227:         <OwnerCard title="App Navigation" icon="🧭">
 228:           <div style={{ display: "grid", gap: 8 }}>
 229:             <Link to="/onboarding">📝 Onboarding</Link>
 230:             <Link to="/owner/morning-brief">🌅 Morning Brief</Link>
 231:               <Link to="/owner/queue-health">🩺 Queue Health</Link>
 232:               <Link to="/owner/search">🔎 Search Everywhere</Link>
 233:               <Link to="/owner/player-progress">👤 Player Progress</Link>
 234:               <Link to="/owner/player-progress-compare">🆚 Player Compare</Link>
 235:               <Link to="/owner/state-achievements">🏆 State Achievements</Link>
 236:               <Link to="/owner/alliance-dashboard-links">🔗 Alliance Dashboard Links</Link>
 237:               <Link to="/dashboard">🧟 My Dashboards</Link>
 238:             <div style={{ fontSize: 12, opacity: 0.8 }}>
 239:               Tip: alliance pages live under <code>/dashboard/&lt;CODE&gt;/calendar</code> and <code>/dashboard/&lt;CODE&gt;/hq-map</code>
 240:             </div>
 241:           </div>
 242:         </OwnerCard>
 243: 
 244:         <OwnerCard title="Health Overview" icon="🧪" right={health.lastRefreshed ? <span style={{ fontSize: 12, opacity: 0.7 }}>refreshed</span> : null}>
 245:           <div style={{ display: "grid", gap: 8 }}>
 246:             <div style={{ display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between", gap: 8 }}>
 247:               <span>Auth session</span>
 248:               {pill(health.sessionUserId ? "OK" : "No session", !!health.sessionUserId)}
 249:             </div>
 250:             <div style={{ display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between", gap: 8 }}>
 251:               <span>Pending requests</span>
 252:               <b>{health.pendingRequests ?? "—"}</b>
 253:             </div>
 254:             <div style={{ display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between", gap: 8 }}>
 255:               <span>Alliances</span>
 256:               <b>{health.alliances ?? "—"}</b>
 257:             </div>
 258:             <div style={{ display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between", gap: 8 }}>
 259:               <span>Players</span>
 260:               <b>{health.players ?? "—"}</b>
 261:             </div>

 263:               <span>Memberships</span>
 264:               <b>{health.memberships ?? "—"}</b>
 265:             </div>
 266:             <div style={{ display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between", gap: 8 }}>
 267:               <span>Events</span>
 268:               <b>{health.events ?? "—"}</b>
 269:             </div>
 270:             <div style={{ display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between", gap: 8 }}>
 271:               <span>Reminders</span>

 273:             </div>

 286:               ))}
 287:             </div>
 288:           ) : null}
 289:

 291:             Note: reminder “activity” updates only when reminders are sent.
 292:           </div>
 293:         </OwnerCard>
 294:       </div>
 295:

 297:       <div style={{ marginTop: 16 }}>
 298:         <OwnerCard title="Alliance Jump Links" icon="🧟‍♂️">
 299:           {alliances.length === 0 ? (
 300:             <div style={{ opacity: 0.75 }}>No alliances found (or RLS blocked).</div>
 301:           ) : (

 303:               {alliances.map((a) => {
 304:                 const enabled = a.enabled !== false;
 305:                 return (
 306:                   <div
 307:                     key={a.code}
 308:                     style={{

 311:                       padding: 10,

 317:                     }}

 320:                       <div style={{ fontWeight: 900 }}>
 321:                         {a.code} {enabled ? "" : <span style={{ fontSize: 12, opacity: 0.7 }}>(disabled)</span>}
 322:                       </div>
 323:                       <div style={{ fontSize: 12, opacity: 0.85 }}>{a.name || a.code}</div>
 324:                     </div>
 325: 
 326:                     <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 10, flexWrap: "wrap" }}>
 327:                       <Link to={`/dashboard/${a.code}/calendar`}>📅 Calendar</Link>
 328:                       <Link to={`/dashboard/${a.code}/guides`}>📚 Guides</Link>
 329:                       <Link to={`/dashboard/${a.code}/hq-map`}>🗺️ HQ Map</Link>
 330:                     </div>
 331:                   </div>
 332:                 );
 333:               })}
 334:             </div>
 335:           )}
 336:         </OwnerCard>
 337:       </div>
 338: 
 339:       {/* Discord Settings Snapshot */}
 340:       <div style={{ marginTop: 16 }}>
 341:         <OwnerCard title="Discord Settings Snapshot (masked)" icon="📣">
 342:           {discord.length === 0 ? (
 343:             <div style={{ opacity: 0.75 }}>
 344:               No discord settings rows found (or RLS blocked). Use <Link to="/dashboard/WOC/discord-webhooks">Discord Settings</Link>.
 345:             </div>
 346:           ) : (
 347:             <div style={{ display: "grid", gap: 10, maxWidth: 1100 }}>
 348:               {discord.map((d, idx) => {
 349:                 const enabled = d.enabled !== false;
 350:                 const id = (d.alliance_id || `row_${idx}`).toUpperCase();
 351:                 const hasHook = !!d.webhook_url && String(d.webhook_url).trim() !== "";
 352:                 return (
 353:                   <div
 354:                     key={`${id}_${idx}`}
 355:                     style={{ border: "1px solid #2a2a2a", borderRadius: 10, padding: 10 }}
 356:                   >
 357:                     <div style={{ display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between", gap: 10, flexWrap: "wrap" }}>
 358:                       <div style={{ fontWeight: 900 }}>{id}</div>
 359:                       <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 8, flexWrap: "wrap" }}>
 360:                         {pill(enabled ? "Enabled" : "Disabled", enabled)}
 361:                         {pill(hasHook ? "Webhook OK" : "Missing webhook", hasHook)}
 362:                       </div>
 363:                     </div>
 364:                     <div style={{ marginTop: 6, fontSize: 12, opacity: 0.85 }}>
 365:                       Webhook: <code>{maskWebhook(d.webhook_url)}</code>
 366:                     </div>

 369:                     </div>

 371:                 );

===== FILE: .\src\pages\owner\OwnerMailBroadcastPage.tsx =====
   1: import React, { useEffect, useState } from "react";
   2: import { useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";
   3: import { supabase } from "../../lib/supabaseBrowserClient";
   4: 
   5: type Kind = "alliance_broadcast" | "state_broadcast";
   6: 
   7: async function copyToClipboard(text: string) {
   8:   try { await navigator.clipboard.writeText(text); alert("Copied"); }
   9:   catch { alert("Copy failed"); }
  10: }
  11: 
  12: export default function OwnerMailBroadcastPage() {
  13:   const nav = useNavigate();
  14:   const [userId, setUserId] = useState<string>("");
  15:   const [kind, setKind] = useState<Kind>("alliance_broadcast");
  16:   const [allianceCode, setAllianceCode] = useState("");
  17:   const [stateCode, setStateCode] = useState("789");
  18:   const [subject, setSubject] = useState("");
  19:   const [body, setBody] = useState("");
  20:   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  21:   const [status, setStatus] = useState("");
  22: 
  23:   useEffect(() => {
  24:     (async () => {
  25:       const { data } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
  26:       setUserId(data.user?.id ?? "");
  27:     })();
  28:   }, []);
  29: 
  30:   async function send() {
  31:     const b = body.trim();
  32:     if (!b) return alert("Body required.");
  33:     if (kind === "alliance_broadcast" && !allianceCode.trim()) return alert("Alliance code required.");
  34:     if (kind === "state_broadcast" && !stateCode.trim()) return alert("State code required.");
  35: 
  36:     setLoading(true);
  37:     setStatus("Sending…");
  38: 
  39:     const payload: any = {
  40:       created_by_user_id: userId,
  41:       kind,
  42:       subject: subject.trim(),
  43:       body: b,
  44:       alliance_code: kind === "alliance_broadcast" ? allianceCode.trim() : null,
  45:       state_code: kind === "state_broadcast" ? stateCode.trim() : null,
  46:     };
  47: 
  48:     const ins = await supabase.from("mail_items").insert(payload).select("*").single();
  49:     if (ins.error) {
  50:       setStatus(ins.error.message);
  51:       setLoading(false);
  52:       return;
  53:     }
  54: 
  55:     setStatus("Sent ✅ (payload copied)");
  56:     window.setTimeout(() => setStatus(""), 1500);
  57: 
  58:     await copyToClipboard(JSON.stringify(ins.data, null, 2));
  59:     setSubject("");
  60:     setBody("");
  61:     setLoading(false);
  62:   }
  63: 
  64:   return (
  65:     <div style={{ padding: 16, maxWidth: 900, margin: "0 auto" }}>
  66:       <div style={{ display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between", gap: 12, flexWrap: "wrap", alignItems: "center" }}>
  67:         <h1 style={{ fontSize: 22, fontWeight: 900, margin: 0 }}>Owner Mail Broadcast</h1>
  68:         <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 8, flexWrap: "wrap" }}>
  69:           <button className="zombie-btn" type="button" onClick={() => nav("/mail")}>Mail Home</button>
  70:           <button className="zombie-btn" type="button" onClick={() => nav("/mail-v2")}>Inbox</button>
  71:           <button className="zombie-btn" type="button" onClick={() => nav("/mail-threads")}>Threads</button>
  72:         </div>
  73:       </div>
  74:       <div style={{ opacity: 0.8, marginTop: 6 }}>
  75:         Creates DB mail items for players to read in <code>/mail-v2</code>. {status ? " • " + status : ""}
  76:       </div>
  77: 
  78:       <div style={{ border: "1px solid #333", borderRadius: 12, overflow: "hidden", marginTop: 12 }}>
  79:         <div style={{ padding: 12, borderBottom: "1px solid #333", fontWeight: 900 }}>Compose</div>
  80:         <div style={{ padding: 12, display: "grid", gap: 10 }}>
  81:           <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 10, flexWrap: "wrap", alignItems: "center" }}>
  82:             <label style={{ opacity: 0.8 }}>Kind</label>
  83:             <select value={kind} onChange={(e) => setKind(e.target.value as Kind)}>
  84:               <option value="alliance_broadcast">alliance broadcast</option>
  85:               <option value="state_broadcast">state broadcast</option>
  86:             </select>
  87: 
  88:             {kind === "alliance_broadcast" ? (
  89:               <>
  90:                 <label style={{ opacity: 0.8 }}>Alliance code</label>
  91:                 <input value={allianceCode} onChange={(e) => setAllianceCode(e.target.value)} placeholder="ex: ABC" />
  92:               </>
  93:             ) : (
  94:               <>
  95:                 <label style={{ opacity: 0.8 }}>State</label>
  96:                 <input value={stateCode} onChange={(e) => setStateCode(e.target.value)} style={{ width: 120 }} />
  97:               </>
  98:             )}
  99:           </div>
 100: 
 101:           <input value={subject} onChange={(e) => setSubject(e.target.value)} placeholder="Subject (optional)..." />
 102:           <textarea value={body} onChange={(e) => setBody(e.target.value)} rows={6} placeholder="Broadcast message..." />
 103: 
 104:           <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 10, justifyContent: "flex-end", flexWrap: "wrap" }}>
 105:             <button onClick={() => copyToClipboard(body)}>Copy body</button>
 106:             <button disabled={loading || !userId} onClick={send}>Send to Mail DB</button>
 107:           </div>
 108:         </div>
 109:       </div>
 110:     </div>
 111:   );
 112: }

===== FILE: .\src\pages\owner\OwnerAllianceDashboardLinksPage.tsx =====
   1: import React, { useEffect, useMemo, useState } from "react";
   2: import { useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";
   3: import CommandCenterShell from "../../components/commandcenter/CommandCenterShell";
   4: import { getCommandCenterModules } from "../../components/commandcenter/ccModules";
   5: import { supabase } from "../../lib/supabaseClient";
   6: 
   7: type AnyRow = any;
   8: 
   9: function s(v: any) {
  10:   return v === null || v === undefined ? "" : String(v);
  11: }
  12: function norm(v: any) {
  13:   return s(v).trim();
  14: }
  15: function normUpper(v: any) {
  16:   return norm(v).toUpperCase();
  17: }
  18: 
  19: const ROLE_OPTIONS = ["owner", "leader", "r4", "r3", "member", "public"];
  20: 
  21: function parseRolesCsv(v: any): string[] {
  22:   return String(v || "").split(",").map((x) => x.trim()).filter(Boolean);
  23: }
  24: 
  25: function rolesToCsv(arr: string[]): string {
  26:   return Array.from(new Set((arr || []).map((x) => String(x || "").trim()).filter(Boolean))).join(",");
  27: }
  28: 
  29: function toggleRoleInCsv(csv: string, role: string): string {
  30:   const current = parseRolesCsv(csv);
  31:   const next = current.includes(role)
  32:     ? current.filter((x) => x !== role)
  33:     : [...current, role];
  34:   return rolesToCsv(next);
  35: }
  36: 
  37: export default function OwnerAllianceDashboardLinksPage() {
  38:   const nav = useNavigate();
  39:   const cc = useMemo(() => getCommandCenterModules(), []);
  40:   const modules = useMemo(() => cc.map(({ key, label, hint }) => ({ key, label, hint })), [cc]);
  41: 
  42:   function onSelectModule(k: string) {
  43:     const to = cc.find((m) => m.key === k)?.to;
  44:     if (to) nav(to);
  45:   }
  46: 
  47:   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  48:   const [status, setStatus] = useState("");
  49:   const [rows, setRows] = useState<AnyRow[]>([]);
  50: 
  51:   const [allianceCode, setAllianceCode] = useState("WOC");
  52:   const [label, setLabel] = useState("");
  53:   const [url, setUrl] = useState("");
  54:   const [sectionName, setSectionName] = useState("");
  55:   const [rolesCsv, setRolesCsv] = useState("");
  56:   const [sort, setSort] = useState("0");
  57:   const [active, setActive] = useState(true);
  58: 
  59:   async function loadAll() {
  60:     try {
  61:       setLoading(true);
  62:       setStatus("");
  63: 
  64:       const r = await supabase
  65:         .from("alliance_dashboard_links")
  66:         .select("*")
  67:         .order("alliance_code", { ascending: true })
  68:         .order("sort", { ascending: true })
  69:         .order("created_at", { ascending: false });
  70: 
  71:       if (r.error) throw r.error;
  72:       setRows((r.data || []) as AnyRow[]);
  73:     } catch (e: any) {
  74:       setStatus(String(e?.message || e || "Load failed"));
  75:     } finally {
  76:       setLoading(false);
  77:     }
  78:   }
  79: 
  80:   useEffect(() => {
  81:     void loadAll();
  82:   }, []);
  83: 
  84:   async function createLink() {
  85:     try {
  86:       if (!normUpper(allianceCode)) return setStatus("Alliance code required.");
  87:       if (!norm(label)) return setStatus("Label required.");
  88:       if (!norm(url)) return setStatus("URL required.");
  89: 
  90:       const ins = await supabase
  91:         .from("alliance_dashboard_links")
  92:         .insert({
  93:           alliance_code: normUpper(allianceCode),
  94:           label: norm(label),
  95:           url: norm(url),
  96:           section_name: norm(sectionName) || null,
  97:           roles_csv: norm(rolesCsv) || null,
  98:           sort: Number(sort || 0),
  99:           active,
 100:         } as any);
 101: 
 102:       if (ins.error) throw ins.error;
 103: 
 104:       setLabel("");
 105:       setUrl("");
 106:       setSectionName("");
 107:       setRolesCsv("");
 108:       setSort("0");
 109:       setActive(true);
 110:       setStatus("Dashboard link created ✅");
 111:       await loadAll();
 112:     } catch (e: any) {
 113:       setStatus("Create failed: " + String(e?.message || e || "unknown error"));
 114:     }
 115:   }
 116: 
 117:   async function saveRow(r: AnyRow) {
 118:     try {
 119:       const up = await supabase
 120:         .from("alliance_dashboard_links")
 121:         .update({
 122:           alliance_code: normUpper(r?.alliance_code),
 123:           label: norm(r?.label),
 124:           url: norm(r?.url),
 125:           section_name: norm(r?.section_name) || null,
 126:           roles_csv: norm(r?.roles_csv) || null,
 127:           sort: Number(r?.sort || 0),
 128:           active: !!r?.active,
 129:         } as any)
 130:         .eq("id", String(r?.id || ""));
 131: 
 132:       if (up.error) throw up.error;
 133: 
 134:       setStatus("Saved ✅");
 135:       await loadAll();
 136:     } catch (e: any) {
 137:       setStatus("Save failed: " + String(e?.message || e || "unknown error"));
 138:     }
 139:   }
 140: 
 141:   async function deleteRow(id: string) {
 142:     try {
 143:       if (!window.confirm("Delete this dashboard link?")) return;
 144: 
 145:       const del = await supabase
 146:         .from("alliance_dashboard_links")
 147:         .delete()
 148:         .eq("id", id);
 149: 
 150:       if (del.error) throw del.error;
 151: 
 152:       setStatus("Deleted ✅");
 153:       await loadAll();
 154:     } catch (e: any) {
 155:       setStatus("Delete failed: " + String(e?.message || e || "unknown error"));
 156:     }
 157:   }
 158: 
 159:   function patchRow(id: string, patch: AnyRow) {
 160:     setRows((prev) => prev.map((x) => String(x?.id || "") === String(id) ? { ...x, ...patch } : x));
 161:   }
 162: 
 163:   return (
 164:     <CommandCenterShell
 165:       title="Owner • Alliance Dashboard Links"
 166:       subtitle="Manage owner-controlled links shown on alliance dashboards"
 167:       modules={modules}
 168:       activeModuleKey="owner"
 169:       onSelectModule={onSelectModule}
 170:       topRight={
 171:         <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 8, flexWrap: "wrap" }}>
 172:           <button className="zombie-btn" type="button" onClick={() => nav("/owner/search")}>Search</button>
 173:           <button className="zombie-btn" type="button" onClick={() => nav("/owner/state-achievements")}>Achievements</button>
 174:           <button className="zombie-btn" type="button" onClick={() => void loadAll()} disabled={loading}>Refresh</button>
 175:         </div>
 176:       }
 177:     >
 178:       {status ? (
 179:         <div style={{ marginBottom: 10, border: "1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.10)", background: "rgba(255,255,255,0.04)", borderRadius: 12, padding: 10 }}>
 180:           {status}
 181:         </div>
 182:       ) : null}
 183: 
 184:       <div className="zombie-card" style={{ marginTop: 12 }}>
 185:         <div style={{ fontWeight: 900, marginBottom: 10 }}>Create Link</div>
 186:         <div style={{ display: "grid", gap: 10 }}>
 187:           <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 10, flexWrap: "wrap" }}>
 188:             <input className="zombie-input" value={allianceCode} onChange={(e) => setAllianceCode(e.target.value)} placeholder="Alliance code" style={{ padding: "10px 12px", width: 140 }} />
 189:             <input className="zombie-input" value={label} onChange={(e) => setLabel(e.target.value)} placeholder="Label" style={{ padding: "10px 12px", minWidth: 220, flex: 1 }} />
 190:             <input className="zombie-input" value={url} onChange={(e) => setUrl(e.target.value)} placeholder="https://..." style={{ padding: "10px 12px", minWidth: 280, flex: 2 }} />
 191:             <input className="zombie-input" value={sectionName} onChange={(e) => setSectionName(e.target.value)} placeholder="Section (Tools, Intel, Ops...)" style={{ padding: "10px 12px", minWidth: 220, flex: 1 }} />
 192:           </div>
 193: 
 194:           <div style={{ display: "grid", gap: 10 }}>
 195:             <input className="zombie-input" value={rolesCsv} onChange={(e) => setRolesCsv(e.target.value)} placeholder="roles_csv (owner,leader,r4)" style={{ padding: "10px 12px", minWidth: 260, flex: 1 }} />
 196: 
 197:             <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 8, flexWrap: "wrap" }}>
 198:               {ROLE_OPTIONS.map((role) => {
 199:                 const checked = parseRolesCsv(rolesCsv).includes(role);
 200:                 return (
 201:                   <label key={role} style={{ display: "flex", gap: 6, alignItems: "center", padding: "6px 10px", borderRadius: 999, border: "1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.10)", background: checked ? "rgba(255,255,255,0.08)" : "transparent" }}>
 202:                     <input
 203:                       type="checkbox"
 204:                       checked={checked}
 205:                       onChange={() => setRolesCsv(toggleRoleInCsv(rolesCsv, role))}
 206:                     />
 207:                     {role}
 208:                   </label>
 209:                 );
 210:               })}
 211:               <button
 212:                 className="zombie-btn"
 213:                 type="button"
 214:                 style={{ padding: "6px 10px" }}
 215:                 onClick={() => setRolesCsv("")}
 216:               >
 217:                 Clear Roles
 218:               </button>
 219:             </div>
 220: 
 221:             <div style={{ fontSize: 12, opacity: 0.7 }}>
 222:               {parseRolesCsv(rolesCsv).length === 0 ? "Visible to all roles" : `Selected roles: ${parseRolesCsv(rolesCsv).join(", ")}`}
 223:             </div>
 224: 
 225:             <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 10, flexWrap: "wrap", alignItems: "center" }}>
 226:               <input className="zombie-input" value={sort} onChange={(e) => setSort(e.target.value)} placeholder="sort" style={{ padding: "10px 12px", width: 100 }} />
 227:               <label style={{ display: "flex", gap: 8, alignItems: "center" }}>
 228:                 <input type="checkbox" checked={active} onChange={(e) => setActive(e.target.checked)} />
 229:                 active
 230:               </label>
 231:               <button className="zombie-btn" type="button" style={{ padding: "10px 12px" }} onClick={() => void createLink()}>
 232:                 Create
 233:               </button>
 234:             </div>
 235:           </div>
 236:         </div>
 237:       </div>
 238: 
 239:       <div className="zombie-card" style={{ marginTop: 12 }}>
 240:         <div style={{ fontWeight: 900, marginBottom: 10 }}>Existing Links</div>
 241:         <div style={{ display: "grid", gap: 10 }}>
 242:           {rows.length === 0 ? <div style={{ opacity: 0.7 }}>No dashboard links yet.</div> : rows.map((r) => (
 243:             <div key={String(r?.id || "")} style={{ padding: 10, borderRadius: 12, border: "1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.10)", background: "rgba(0,0,0,0.20)" }}>
 244:               <div style={{ display: "grid", gap: 10 }}>
 245:                 <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 10, flexWrap: "wrap" }}>
 246:                   <input className="zombie-input" value={String(r?.alliance_code || "")} onChange={(e) => patchRow(r.id, { alliance_code: e.target.value })} style={{ padding: "8px 10px", width: 140 }} />
 247:                   <input className="zombie-input" value={String(r?.label || "")} onChange={(e) => patchRow(r.id, { label: e.target.value })} style={{ padding: "8px 10px", minWidth: 220, flex: 1 }} />
 248:                   <input className="zombie-input" value={String(r?.url || "")} onChange={(e) => patchRow(r.id, { url: e.target.value })} style={{ padding: "8px 10px", minWidth: 280, flex: 2 }} />
 249:                   <input className="zombie-input" value={String(r?.section_name || "")} onChange={(e) => patchRow(r.id, { section_name: e.target.value })} placeholder="Section" style={{ padding: "8px 10px", minWidth: 180, flex: 1 }} />
 250:                 </div>
 251: 
 252:                 <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 10, flexWrap: "wrap", alignItems: "center" }}>
 253:                   <div style={{ minWidth: 240, flex: 1 }}>
 254:                     <input className="zombie-input" value={String(r?.roles_csv || "")} onChange={(e) => patchRow(r.id, { roles_csv: e.target.value })} placeholder="roles_csv" style={{ padding: "8px 10px", width: "100%" }} />
 255: 
 256:                     <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 8, flexWrap: "wrap", marginTop: 8 }}>
 257:                       {ROLE_OPTIONS.map((role) => {
 258:                         const checked = parseRolesCsv(r?.roles_csv).includes(role);
 259:                         return (
 260:                           <label key={role} style={{ display: "flex", gap: 6, alignItems: "center", padding: "4px 8px", borderRadius: 999, border: "1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.10)", background: checked ? "rgba(255,255,255,0.08)" : "transparent" }}>
 261:                             <input
 262:                               type="checkbox"
 263:                               checked={checked}
 264:                               onChange={() => patchRow(r.id, { roles_csv: toggleRoleInCsv(String(r?.roles_csv || ""), role) })}
 265:                             />
 266:                             {role}
 267:                           </label>
 268:                         );
 269:                       })}
 270: 
 271:                       <button
 272:                         className="zombie-btn"
 273:                         type="button"
 274:                         style={{ padding: "4px 8px", fontSize: 12 }}
 275:                         onClick={() => patchRow(r.id, { roles_csv: "" })}
 276:                       >
 277:                         Clear Roles
 278:                       </button>
 279:                     </div>
 280: 
 281:                     <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 6, flexWrap: "wrap", marginTop: 6 }}>
 282:                       {parseRolesCsv(r?.roles_csv).length === 0 ? <span style={{ opacity: 0.65, fontSize: 12 }}>Visible to all roles</span> : parseRolesCsv(r?.roles_csv).map((role) => (
 283:                         <span key={role} style={{ fontSize: 12, padding: "4px 8px", borderRadius: 999, border: "1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.10)" }}>{role}</span>
 284:                       ))}
 285:                     </div>
 286:                   </div>
 287:                   <input className="zombie-input" value={String(r?.sort ?? 0)} onChange={(e) => patchRow(r.id, { sort: e.target.value })} style={{ padding: "8px 10px", width: 100 }} />
 288:                   <label style={{ display: "flex", gap: 8, alignItems: "center" }}>
 289:                     <input type="checkbox" checked={!!r?.active} onChange={(e) => patchRow(r.id, { active: e.target.checked })} />
 290:                     active
 291:                   </label>
 292:                   <a className="zombie-btn" href={String(r?.url || "#")} target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" style={{ padding: "8px 10px", textDecoration: "none" }}>Preview</a>
 293:                   <button className="zombie-btn" type="button" style={{ padding: "8px 10px" }} onClick={() => void saveRow(r)}>Save</button>
 294:                   <button className="zombie-btn" type="button" style={{ padding: "8px 10px" }} onClick={() => void deleteRow(String(r?.id || ""))}>Delete</button>
 295:                 </div>
 296:               </div>
 297:             </div>
 298:           ))}
 299:         </div>
 300:       </div>
 301:     </CommandCenterShell>
 302:   );
 303: }

===== FILE: .\src\components\dashboard\AllianceDashboardLinksPanel.tsx =====
   1: import React, { useEffect, useMemo, useState } from "react";
   2: import { supabase } from "../../lib/supabaseClient";
   3: 
   4: type AnyRow = any;
   5: 
   6: function s(v: any) {
   7:   return v === null || v === undefined ? "" : String(v);
   8: }
   9: function norm(v: any) {
  10:   return s(v).trim();
  11: }
  12: function normLower(v: any) {
  13:   return norm(v).toLowerCase();
  14: }
  15: 
  16: function roleAllowed(rolesCsv: string | null | undefined, userRole: string | null | undefined) {
  17:   const csv = normLower(rolesCsv);
  18:   if (!csv) return true;
  19:   const role = normLower(userRole);
  20:   if (!role) return false;
  21:   const allowed = csv.split(",").map((x) => x.trim()).filter(Boolean);
  22:   return allowed.includes(role);
  23: }
  24: 
  25: export default function AllianceDashboardLinksPanel(props: { allianceCode: string; userRole?: string | null; title?: string }) {
  26:   const allianceCode = norm(props.allianceCode).toUpperCase();
  27:   const userRole = norm(props.userRole || "");
  28:   const title = norm(props.title || "Alliance Links");
  29: 
  30:   const [rows, setRows] = useState<AnyRow[]>([]);
  31:   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  32: 
  33:   async function loadAll() {
  34:     try {
  35:       setLoading(true);
  36: 
  37:       const r = await supabase
  38:         .from("alliance_dashboard_links")
  39:         .select("*")
  40:         .eq("alliance_code", allianceCode)
  41:         .eq("active", true)
  42:         .order("sort", { ascending: true })
  43:         .order("label", { ascending: true });
  44: 
  45:       if (!r.error) setRows((r.data || []) as AnyRow[]);
  46:       else setRows([]);
  47:     } finally {
  48:       setLoading(false);
  49:     }
  50:   }
  51: 
  52:   useEffect(() => {
  53:     if (!allianceCode) return;
  54:     void loadAll();
  55:   }, [allianceCode]);
  56: 
  57:   const visibleRows = useMemo(() => {
  58:     return rows.filter((r) => roleAllowed(String(r?.roles_csv || ""), userRole));
  59:   }, [rows, userRole]);
  60: 
  61:   const groupedRows = useMemo(() => {
  62:     const map = new Map<string, AnyRow[]>();
  63:     for (const r of visibleRows) {
  64:       const section = norm(r?.section_name || "General");
  65:       if (!map.has(section)) map.set(section, []);
  66:       map.get(section)!.push(r);
  67:     }
  68:     return Array.from(map.entries()).sort((a, b) => a[0].localeCompare(b[0]));
  69:   }, [visibleRows]);
  70: 
  71:   if (!allianceCode) return null;
  72: 
  73:   return (
  74:     <div className="zombie-card" style={{ marginTop: 12 }}>
  75:       <div style={{ fontWeight: 900, marginBottom: 10 }}>{title}</div>
  76:       {loading ? <div style={{ opacity: 0.7 }}>Loading…</div> : null}
  77:       {!loading && visibleRows.length === 0 ? <div style={{ opacity: 0.7 }}>No links available.</div> : null}
  78: 
  79:       <div style={{ display: "grid", gap: 12 }}>
  80:         {groupedRows.map(([section, links]) => (
  81:           <div key={section}>
  82:             <div style={{ fontSize: 12, opacity: 0.7, marginBottom: 6 }}>{section}</div>
  83:             <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 8, flexWrap: "wrap" }}>
  84:               {links.map((r) => (
  85:                 <a
  86:                   key={String(r?.id || "")}
  87:                   className="zombie-btn"
  88:                   href={String(r?.url || "#")}
  89:                   target="_blank"
  90:                   rel="noreferrer"
  91:                   style={{ padding: "10px 12px", textDecoration: "none" }}
  92:                 >
  93:                   {String(r?.label || "Link")}
  94:                 </a>
  95:               ))}
  96:             </div>
  97:           </div>
  98:         ))}
  99:       </div>
 100:     </div>
 101:   );
 102: }
 103: 

===== FILE: .\src\pages\alliance\AllianceDashboardHomePage.tsx =====
   1: import AllianceDashboardLinksPanel from "../../components/dashboard/AllianceDashboardLinksPanel";
   2: import React from "react";
   3: import { useParams } from "react-router-dom";
   4: import InnerDashboardHomeImported from "../PlayerDashboardPage";
   5: // FROM_APPROUTES: detected default dashboard home component
   6: InnerDashboardHome = InnerDashboardHomeImported;
   7: 
   8: /**
   9:  * This page exists ONLY to safely add non-fragile UI on the alliance dashboard home route:
  10:  *   /dashboard/:alliance_id
  11:  *
  12:  * It renders Quick Links + the existing dashboard home component.
  13:  *
  14:  * NOTE: AppRoutes will be patched to wrap the existing element with this page.
  15:  */
  16: 
  17: // The "InnerDashboardHome" import will be injected by AppRoutes patch if possible.
  18: // Fallback: if the import cannot be determined, we'll render only the Quick Links.
  19: let InnerDashboardHome: any = null;
  20: 
  21: export default function AllianceDashboardHomePage() {
  22:   const { alliance_id } = useParams();
  23:   const code = (alliance_id || "").toString().toUpperCase();
  24: 
  25:   return (
  26:     <div>
  27: {InnerDashboardHome ? <InnerDashboardHome key={code} /> : null}
  28:     </div>
  29:   );
  30: }
